< Text>
False advertising! Very disappointing experience with Katzkin.

I really wanted cooled seats on my next car, but I didn't want to pay thousands more for the higher trim level that included that option (and I didn't want all the other stuff included in that trim). Then I found Katzkin. Their website has a page dedicated to the car I wanted, and the "Design Your Seats" drop down boxes also had options for my car. I even emailed them to double check that I could get cooled seats in a certain design. They said yes! So, I bought the car I wanted in a lower trim level, and after that I contacted Katzkin again to finalize my purchase of the seats.

Only THEN was I told that no, they actually don't have the right pattern for my car.

So, do yourself a favor and don't trust Katzkin's website. Don't trust the sales reps either.  Ask to speak directly to the pattern department before making any decisions. That's apparently the only way to know for sure.< /Text>

Kyle Roberts (Krobear Diderot)< /name>
<Time>1501817721547< /Time>< rating>
1</rating>
<Text>I was told by Chase Chevrolet that Katzkin leather products were far superior to factory leather. I was assured that Katzkin was not only a great alternative but the quality far surpassed that of the factory leather. The days leading up to me receiving my truck back from the installer were filled with angst as I saw online several finished products with tons of wrinkles in the leather as if the leather were loose, a condition I had never seen on a factory GM leather interior. My vehicle prior to this was a 99 Escalade and even it did not have such wrinkles. When I picked up my truck up my fears were confirmed, these wrinkles were there, albeit not as bad as in some pictures, however they were there. It looked nothing like the tight jobs advertised by Katzkin. After further inspection I realized that it was simply due to the fact that Katzkin is not a leather interior but merely seat cover secured by zippers and velcro. At this point I definitely regretted the decision to have Katzkin installed. I felt lied to by the dealership and by the ads, Katzkin is nowhere near a factory job. It may have a higher leather content but it is clearly aftermarket, not in a positive way. This "Higher Quality" alternative is simply a ploy to get people already shelling out thousands on a new car to pony up another thousand dollars or so for SEAT COVERS.
So at this point I regret the purchase but oh well, I wanted leather, it saved me about 500 bux vs. going factory and if it gets messed up its relatively cheap to replace compared to doing a real leather upholstery. What I am gonna do, ask them to put the cloth interior back in? I decide that it'll work, and stop worrying about it. That is until today. I got out of my truck and noticed that the black leather is already wearing off. A condition generally reserved for vehicles with thousands of miles on it. I have 350 miles on my truck, 100 were put on with the Katzkin installed. I do not keep keys in my back pocket, I throw my wallet on the center console before i get in so I don't sit on it, there is absolutely nothing that should of caused this wear other than poor quality. I have had this leather for maybe two weeks now and I can only imagine what it ill look like in 6 months, a year, in 3 years. It is literally wearing like a cheap Pleather office chair but faster. I registered for my warranty immediately and read after registering that Katzkin will not honor the warranty for wear. I intend on contacting them tomorrow to see if they will iron this out as the leather is so new but after all of the lies up to this point I have very little confidence that they will do much to rectify the situation.</Text>< pics>

One truck we were never given a title to and had to be returned, after 4 months! This alone caused our company a great amount of downtime. That same truck had problems from the start. Dead batteries, oil line was rigged together and caused a large oil leak through our customers parking lot (first time out in the truck). Missing pieces in the cab, lift gate wouldn't go down due to poor install, VERY rusty (rust started coming through the new paint EVERYWHERE in the first few days). Box was caved in and leaked water on our tools. The truck also went into limp mode saying it had a major fuel leak, this is within 100 miles of getting the truck.

The 2nd truck had a broken rear spring pack making the truck drive sideways down the road, bad enough for random witnesses to call and say one of our trucks is going to tip over. The fuel injectors were bad, causing the exhaust system to "regen" too often, throwing a code within the first 100 miles. The "recall" work was never performed. I'm sure there is more.

The 3rd truck, this was the truck that replaced the truck without a title. It was sold as "clean air certified" but it blew black clouds of smoke the first time we started it. Come to find out, the exhaust system was completely ruined and was no longer functioning. This was a MAJOR repair costing 10k!

So far we are out 15k on repairs to our trucks, these trucks should have never been sent out with all these issues. We were scammed. Fam Vans is now dodging us and is not taking any responsibility.

Honestly, there is even more complaints and problems we have had but I think you get the idea. If you are making a purchase that your livelihood depends on, be careful, don't trust Fam Vans.<//Text>< userid>

< Time>
1547173450950< /Time>
<Rate>5<//Rate>< Text>
I've been all around California (and the rest the U.S.); this is still the best menudo I can find.

First thing -- most important -- Rosa Maria's restaurant only serves their menudo on the weekend; this is one of the main ways to tell if a business prepares their menudo fresh or simply reheats a frozen stock.

The tripe used is the reticulum section, or "honeycomb", the best type of meat for the stew -- no grease, no gristle. They boil away the fat, ensuring the meat and stock aren't oily and clouded, add the most tender hominy and give it the time it requires to properly stew.

By the time it makes its way to you, this menudo's been properly seasoned and the additional spices and trimmings the staff provide simply make an already amazing dish even more mouthwatering. To top it all off, they'll even add a meaty, tender pork bone, the perfect way to finish off such a satisfying meal.

This place is excellent. Sometimes, the beans have little rocks, but that's just another sign of freshness.

Keep it up, Rosa Maria's! I'll see you next Saturday!< /Text>
